(<code>kubectl.kubernetes.io/last-applied-configuration</code>).</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8037-8b60-f357e70bd034"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80fd-9ca6-fd9a9a52f653" class=""><strong>Analogy</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80d5-9ab9-d83b345627d0" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><code>create</code> = <strong>adding a new book to a shelf üìö</strong> (fails if the book already exists)</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80b4-a5ba-e6253394bb27" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><code>apply</code> = <strong>updating or adding a book to a shelf üìñ</strong> (creates if missing, updates if exists)</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-806a-9c08-e9290088a59e"/><p id="272378cb-b17f-80e7-a6e9-f9378b885da0" class="">‚úÖ <strong>One-liner interview answer:</strong></p><p id="272378cb-b17f-8070-92bf-d6ca8343ea0e" class=""><em><code>kubectl create</code></em><em> creates a new resource and fails if it exists, while </em><em><code>kubectl apply</code></em><em> is declarative and idempotent, creating or updating resources as needed.</em></p></details></li></ul><ul id="26b378cb-b17f-80af-9edd-ff7a3ec932e9" class="toggle"><li><details open=""><summary><strong>Question 81:</strong> How does Kubernetes handle scaling of applications?</summary><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8066-a642-d3585f93370d" class=""><strong>Kubernetes Scaling</strong></h3><p id="272378cb-b17f-8065-826b-f5e310917893" class="">Kubernetes can scale applications by <strong>adjusting the number of Pods</strong> running for a Deployment, ReplicaSet, or StatefulSet. Scaling can be <strong>manual</strong> or <strong>automatic</strong>.</p><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80a7-bc3e-e1234e86e3ae"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-801f-9322-c96d94dc610c" class=""><strong>1. Manual Scaling</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-806b-b1e6-d535617246f9" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Adjust the number of replicas for a Deployment or ReplicaSet manually:</li></ul><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8088-a6d2-ece4f483828b" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl scale deployment my-app --replicas=5

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-808d-a71b-c3529f787f2f" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">The scheduler will <strong>create or terminate Pods</strong> to match the desired count.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8072-aa48-eec0035cb0a7"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80db-bebe-e15c0fabfd0a" class=""><strong>2. Horizontal Pod Autoscaler (HPA)</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80f2-8a3c-ce53d240550f" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>Automatically scales Pods horizontally</strong> based on CPU, memory, or custom metrics.</li></ul><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8060-8bf9-edc0d6f083e4" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl autoscale deployment my-app --cpu-percent=50 --min=2 --max=10

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-806a-86a2-f32231098ec1" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Example:<ul id="272378cb-b17f-805b-a699-f509684c466f" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:circle">If CPU usage &gt; 50%, HPA adds more Pods.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80c7-834a-caf190373d6b" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:circle">If CPU usage &lt; threshold, HPA reduces Pods.</li></ul></li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8004-94b6-d737e86c0c4b"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80bc-90ff-f5af1435c079" class=""><strong>3. Vertical Pod Autoscaler (VPA)</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80f2-a335-ecce9e4806c3" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>Automatically adjusts CPU and memory requests</strong> of Pods.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80fe-a515-f0ad75f6c261" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Helps when workloads require <strong>more resources instead of more Pods</strong>.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8006-b83d-e6176a61cf45"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8083-8622-ff31df00cedb" class=""><strong>4. Cluster Autoscaler</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80fc-acb8-f991d53a4492" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>Scales the number of nodes</strong> in the cluster based on resource requirements.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80e0-a977-e22252fbf40d" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Works together with HPA to ensure <strong>sufficient node resources</strong> for scheduled Pods.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8068-9d05-d4d06b7f84e9"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8070-b508-e4397a6bd098" class=""><strong>Key Points</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80d1-a326-c191e0326e3c" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Scaling is based on <strong>desired state</strong>; Kubernetes reconciles actual state automatically.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8029-94a0-dd68715623d7" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">HPA = <strong>scale Pods horizontally</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8029-ba4f-e215738592a1" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">VPA = <strong>scale Pods vertically</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80fe-8d7c-d750b15f8d21" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Cluster Autoscaler = <strong>scale nodes</strong></li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8017-9b54-f999bebe3ea4"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-806b-b9dc-f8a962dd092d" class=""><strong>Analogy</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-808f-8bca-c4c995714382" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Manual scaling = <strong>adding more chairs for guests ü™ë</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-803b-9437-e98dbb3dab48" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">HPA = <strong>automatic chairs added when more guests arrive</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8073-9fd3-e9a1eee6171d" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">VPA = <strong>making chairs bigger for comfort</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-801d-87f0-ea3568b03a4a" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Cluster Autoscaler = <strong>adding more tables to fit extra chairs</strong></li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80b0-8207-dcfe9883758b"/><p id="272378cb-b17f-8080-947e-eaef45e278a4" class="">‚úÖ <strong>One-liner interview answer:</strong></p><p id="272378cb-b17f-8041-8d01-f2466f60358a" class=""><em>Kubernetes handles scaling by adjusting the number of Pods (manual or HPA), adjusting Pod resources (VPA), and scaling cluster nodes (Cluster Autoscaler) to maintain the desired state of applications.</em></p></details></li></ul><ul id="26b378cb-b17f-80c9-a651-c0066e6be32c" class="toggle"><li><details open=""><summary><strong>Question 82:</strong> What is the purpose of a <code>Kubernetes Service Account</code>?</summary><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-806a-b2ee-cc56f728916a" class=""><strong>Kubernetes Service Account</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8063-80ba-f67e236f7c3f" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">A <strong>Service Account (SA)</strong> provides an <strong>identity for Pods</strong> to interact with the Kubernetes API.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8056-afc3-d366d534eee4" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Pods can <strong>use Service Accounts to authenticate</strong> when accessing cluster resources instead of using a user‚Äôs credentials.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-801e-8357-ed5f171c15eb"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80b0-9347-e4da3b8c803b" class=""><strong>Key Points</strong></h3><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-805e-baa8-f06038a52991" class="numbered-list" start="1"><li><strong>Authentication</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80ac-b2f0-fe46eb6d354b" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Each Pod can mount a <strong>token associated with a Service Account</strong>.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8034-a6fc-e8158e4bacb5" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Token is used for <strong>API requests to the Kubernetes API server</strong>.</li></ul></li></ol><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-8063-8cad-c0fc938ab95d" class="numbered-list" start="2"><li><strong>Default Service Account</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80b1-9e2e-ef8e961b76eb" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Every namespace has a <strong>default Service Account</strong>.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8086-b9f0-faf94d2c252e" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Pods automatically use it if no other SA is specified.</li></ul></li></ol><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-8058-87fa-edc9ede72f2c" class="numbered-list" start="3"><li><strong>Custom Service Accounts</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80f7-90d2-c75d7da5f949" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">You can create <strong>custom Service Accounts</strong> with specific <strong>RBAC roles and permissions</strong>.</li></ul><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-804d-89c8-c06fdc6d6f15" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">apiVersion: v1
kind: ServiceAccount
metadata:
  name: my-app-sa

</code></pre></li></ol><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-806c-922e-fbb33b91e288" class="numbered-list" start="4"><li><strong>RBAC Integration</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8030-ad3a-c493fb61b571" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Combine Service Accounts with <strong>Roles or ClusterRoles</strong> to control access.</li></ul><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8012-a62a-ecee31d86088" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kind: RoleBinding
apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
metadata:
  name: read-pods
subjects:
- kind: ServiceAccount
  name: my-app-sa
roleRef:
  kind: Role
  name: pod-reader
  apiGroup: rbac.authorization.k8s.io

</code></pre></li></ol><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8073-9e32-d6a1879e179c"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80b2-9905-ee5d8845945b" class=""><strong>Use Cases</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8024-9fe5-d08e410baf29" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Pods accessing the <strong>Kubernetes API securely</strong>.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80c1-a36d-d374d2189b13" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Assigning <strong>least privilege access</strong> to applications.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8067-ad6f-ca68a633f935" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Integrating with <strong>external secrets or cloud provider APIs</strong>.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8053-a4a5-d9e2bb560a2c"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80cc-a738-cea1e7a62ace" class=""><strong>Analogy</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8025-ad56-ef157be4f757" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Service Account = <strong>employee ID badge üÜî</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8049-ac0e-d68ac25f6471" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:circle">Allows the Pod to access certain rooms (API resources) based on permissions assigned.</li></ul></li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8058-bb84-e54112d2b60b"/><p id="272378cb-b17f-803c-b602-ca603e5e1566" class="">‚úÖ <strong>One-liner interview answer:</strong></p><p id="272378cb-b17f-80af-8e19-d1dc684bf334" class=""><em>A Kubernetes Service Account provides an identity for Pods to authenticate with the API server, enabling secure and controlled access to cluster resources, often combined with RBAC for fine-grained permissions.</em></p></details></li></ul><ul id="26b378cb-b17f-80be-887c-ce3ba5bce021" class="toggle"><li><details open=""><summary><strong>Question 83:</strong> Explain the concept of <code>Kubernetes RBAC</code> (Role-Based Access Control).</summary><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80c5-acff-d18a4ac7e29f" class=""><strong>Kubernetes RBAC (Role-Based Access Control)</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80fb-b104-e973e57f7904" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">RBAC allows administrators to <strong>control who can perform what actions on which resources</strong> in a Kubernetes cluster.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80a7-8b22-ea764b5f1c45" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Uses <strong>roles and bindings</strong> to enforce permissions.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-804d-b926-f2b97ab8c832"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-803c-9d2f-e7196ad0c011" class=""><strong>Key Components</strong></h3><table id="272378cb-b17f-804a-bb40-d0dab8cc555e" class="simple-table"><thead class="simple-table-header"><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8092-8243-d8d66f54dc28"><th id="QxO&lt;" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header"><strong>Component</strong></th><th id="&gt;ciI" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header"><strong>Description</strong></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr id="272378cb-b17f-80e6-981b-e5b818346c56"><td id="QxO&lt;" class=""><strong>Role</strong></td><td id="&gt;ciI" class="">Defines <strong>permissions within a namespace</strong> (verbs like get, list, create) for resources like Pods, Services, etc.</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8098-86c5-e4bd3b392465"><td id="QxO&lt;" class=""><strong>ClusterRole</strong></td><td id="&gt;ciI" class="">Defines <strong>permissions cluster-wide</strong> (across all namespaces).</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-802d-ba7b-c2b5f5453dd5"><td id="QxO&lt;" class=""><strong>RoleBinding</strong></td><td id="&gt;ciI" class="">Assigns a Role to a <strong>user, group, or service account</strong> within a namespace.</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-80c3-ab3e-d2e4d4536953"><td id="QxO&lt;" class=""><strong>ClusterRoleBinding</strong></td><td id="&gt;ciI" class="">Assigns a ClusterRole to a <strong>user, group, or service account</strong> across the cluster.</td></tr></tbody></table><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80c8-a9e9-fe4e00a1949f"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8077-84dd-f54fbe727d1e" class=""><strong>Example Role</strong></h3><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80af-b78f-e04e291ee4a3" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
kind: Role
metadata:
  namespace: dev
  name: pod-reader
rules:
- apiGroups: [&quot;&quot;]
  resources: [&quot;pods&quot;]
  verbs: [&quot;get&quot;, &quot;watch&quot;, &quot;list&quot;]

</code></pre><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-808b-ae53-c383500d7caa" class=""><strong>Example RoleBinding</strong></h3><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-804d-848b-c5e2916180d5" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
kind: RoleBinding
metadata:
  name: read-pods-binding
  namespace: dev
subjects:
- kind: ServiceAccount
  name: my-app-sa
  namespace: dev
roleRef:
  kind: Role
  name: pod-reader
  apiGroup: rbac.authorization.k8s.io

</code></pre><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8085-99c9-d9d931e9a685"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8075-a3cd-f4ea17e2af19" class=""><strong>Key Points</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8021-b363-c02c1c994c11" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">RBAC is <strong>namespace-aware</strong>, allowing fine-grained access control.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80c1-928f-dd1de2e31ee1" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Service Accounts, users, or groups are <strong>assigned roles</strong> to access resources.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8093-bcbd-f1b64ff7b3d3" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Helps enforce <strong>least privilege</strong> and <strong>secure cluster operations</strong>.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8024-bfa2-c9dd81f95d44"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80b5-aaf5-e1005b41d948" class=""><strong>Analogy</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8020-9949-cb52177e7af2" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">RBAC = <strong>access control cards in an office üè¢</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-809e-87ba-e6e77a4d360e" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:circle">Each employee (user/SA) can access only rooms (resources) they are authorized to enter.</li></ul></li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8053-b0ce-dc923ebc7249"/><p id="272378cb-b17f-80c6-a1b6-c991d3844283" class="">‚úÖ <strong>One-liner interview answer:</strong></p><p id="272378cb-b17f-80af-87c9-da559c784e72" class=""><em>Kubernetes RBAC is a system for controlling access to resources by assigning roles with specific permissions to users, groups, or service accounts, enabling fine-grained and secure access control in the cluster.</em></p></details></li></ul><ul id="26b378cb-b17f-8029-b5a7-fd74e8850384" class="toggle"><li><details open=""><summary><strong>Question 84:</strong> What is the difference between <code>Kubernetes deployment</code> and <code>Kubernetes statefulset</code>?</summary><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80f7-b051-d3e5cc03d321" class=""><strong>Kubernetes Deployment vs StatefulSet</strong></h3><table id="272378cb-b17f-8082-b685-e6f07b65ae75" class="simple-table"><thead class="simple-table-header"><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8042-a915-f4216308fb8a"><th id="DZ;J" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header"><strong>Aspect</strong></th><th id="v[J&lt;" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header" style="width:264px"><strong>Deployment</strong></th><th id="GIGV" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header" style="width:278px"><strong>StatefulSet</strong></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr id="272378cb-b17f-80d5-923f-d193507c9246"><td id="DZ;J" class=""><strong>Use Case</strong></td><td id="v[J&lt;" class="" style="width:264px">Stateless applications</td><td id="GIGV" class="" style="width:278px">Stateful applications (databases, queues, etc.)</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8044-b48c-d91185c0b456"><td id="DZ;J" class=""><strong>Pod Identity</strong></td><td id="v[J&lt;" class="" style="width:264px">Pods are <strong>interchangeable</strong>; no stable identity</td><td id="GIGV" class="" style="width:278px">Pods have <strong>stable, unique identities</strong> (hostname &amp; network)</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8056-9e54-e56d5eebc2d2"><td id="DZ;J" class=""><strong>Pod Naming</strong></td><td id="v[J&lt;" class="" style="width:264px">Randomly generated names</td><td id="GIGV" class="" style="width:278px">Predictable names: <code>&lt;statefulset-name&gt;-&lt;ordinal&gt;</code></td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-80d8-9430-f318a0cbe40d"><td id="DZ;J" class=""><strong>Storage</strong></td><td id="v[J&lt;" class="" style="width:264px">Usually ephemeral or shared storage</td><td id="GIGV" class="" style="width:278px">Persistent storage per Pod using PersistentVolumeClaims (PVCs)</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8072-9b7a-f1efd8173213"><td id="DZ;J" class=""><strong>Scaling</strong></td><td id="v[J&lt;" class="" style="width:264px">Easy; Pods can be added or removed arbitrarily</td><td id="GIGV" class="" style="width:278px">Pods scaled in order; one Pod is created/terminated at a time</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-802c-b013-e37c338d5df6"><td id="DZ;J" class=""><strong>Update Strategy</strong></td><td id="v[J&lt;" class="" style="width:264px">RollingUpdate or Recreate</td><td id="GIGV" class="" style="width:278px">RollingUpdate or OnDelete (controlled updates)</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-802c-8296-f563aa48382a"><td id="DZ;J" class=""><strong>Networking</strong></td><td id="v[J&lt;" class="" style="width:264px">No stable network ID</td><td id="GIGV" class="" style="width:278px">Each Pod gets a <strong>stable network identity</strong></td></tr></tbody></table><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8030-b2c3-e55884491a85"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8075-bdc8-c738bc19f1e2" class=""><strong>Key Points</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8091-a0a7-f9b09108372a" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>Deployment</strong> = Best for stateless apps like web servers, APIs.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-801a-8083-f5c772a869bc" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>StatefulSet</strong> = Best for stateful apps that need <strong>stable storage and identity</strong>, like databases (MySQL, Kafka).</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8018-be4a-d567db873bae" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">StatefulSets maintain <strong>ordered deployment, scaling, and termination</strong>.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-802a-a6bf-f8f8ac4838b0"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80ea-9386-d660cee1fbd0" class=""><strong>Analogy</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80d2-9252-f333a86b0cd4" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Deployment = <strong>identical robots ü§ñ</strong> (any one can replace another)</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80ca-a2a1-e33a82a04b4f" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">StatefulSet = <strong>employees with personal desks üßë‚Äçüíª</strong> (each has a unique identity and workspace)</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80ca-a6e7-f808f39db276"/><p id="272378cb-b17f-80ca-a249-d4f30546bead" class="">‚úÖ <strong>One-liner interview answer:</strong></p><p id="272378cb-b17f-8004-9be2-d537b9e77ad0" class=""><em>A Deployment manages stateless Pods with interchangeable identities, while a StatefulSet manages stateful Pods with stable identities, persistent storage, and ordered deployment and scaling.</em></p></details></li></ul><ul id="26b378cb-b17f-8041-9972-f23781d8d64a" class="toggle"><li><details open=""><summary><strong>Question 85:</strong> How do you manage storage in Kubernetes with Persistent Volumes?</summary><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-806f-b6fc-f2a784bd3945" class=""><strong>Managing Storage in Kubernetes with Persistent Volumes</strong></h3><p id="272378cb-b17f-80c5-9597-d16c0a6a8129" class="">Kubernetes separates <strong>storage management</strong> from Pods using <strong>Persistent Volumes (PV)</strong> and <strong>Persistent Volume Claims (PVC)</strong>.</p><hr id="272378cb-b17f-808d-91f9-f50403e14f4c"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-805c-b517-fcc5566bd752" class=""><strong>Key Concepts</strong></h3><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-80ad-9b4c-f8a99ba2d029" class="numbered-list" start="1"><li><strong>PersistentVolume (PV)</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80b1-854a-c9fd1bde48de" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Cluster-level storage resource <strong>provisioned by an admin or dynamically</strong>.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-800a-8e7c-de894d2804a4" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Represents actual storage (NFS, AWS EBS, GCE PD, local disk).</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8009-9473-cd55e8c08b47" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Has <strong>capacity, access modes, and reclaim policy</strong>.</li></ul></li></ol><p id="272378cb-b17f-80d6-9365-ec0a49d3105f" class=""><strong>Example PV</strong></p><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8024-9fd7-cc5c597de0d3" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">apiVersion: v1
kind: PersistentVolume
metadata:
  name: pv-data
spec:
  capacity:
    storage: 10Gi
  accessModes:
    - ReadWriteOnce
  persistentVolumeReclaimPolicy: Retain
  hostPath:
    path: &quot;/mnt/data&quot;

</code></pre><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-80a2-980b-e26b1ceebc42" class="numbered-list" start="1"><li><strong>PersistentVolumeClaim (PVC)</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-800f-aa9f-c19009d7adce" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Pod-level request for storage.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-801c-a1b7-c890d077350d" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Specifies <strong>size and access mode</strong> required.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-800e-b4ad-c44000b5d6a0" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Kubernetes <strong>binds PVC to a matching PV</strong> automatically.</li></ul></li></ol><p id="272378cb-b17f-803f-8c70-e5d5ac6a7bc5" class=""><strong>Example PVC</strong></p><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80e0-bc61-d55781272b9d" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">apiVersion: v1
kind: PersistentVolumeClaim
metadata:
  name: pvc-data
spec:
  accessModes:
    - ReadWriteOnce
  resources:
    requests:
      storage: 5Gi

</code></pre><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-80fe-96e7-ce536804a657" class="numbered-list" start="1"><li><strong>Using PVC in a Pod</strong></li></ol><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8036-ab19-fdb5e46da7f2" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">apiVersion: v1
kind: Pod
metadata:
  name: my-pod
spec:
  containers:
  - name: app
    image: nginx
    volumeMounts:
    - mountPath: &quot;/usr/share/nginx/html&quot;
      name: storage
  volumes:
  - name: storage
    persistentVolumeClaim:
      claimName: pvc-data

</code></pre><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80db-9ff6-dbca2de8798b"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80ee-a77a-fc8e4a2337f5" class=""><strong>Access Modes</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8019-b007-cdb4a1c71026" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>ReadWriteOnce (RWO)</strong> ‚Üí Mounted by a single node</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8049-9b33-cfaca9c0cc8c" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>ReadOnlyMany (ROX)</strong> ‚Üí Mounted read-only by multiple nodes</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8009-8fd2-caccc6a5644f" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>ReadWriteMany (RWX)</strong> ‚Üí Mounted read/write by multiple nodes</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8021-8465-f14d6188019d"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8042-b2ba-ee0ab8e2bd7e" class=""><strong>Reclaim Policies</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-802b-8774-c0d17c2b45c4" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>Retain</strong> ‚Üí Keep data after PVC deletion</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80fe-9628-fe76c1c858cd" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>Recycle</strong> ‚Üí Clear data and make PV available again</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80ae-bff0-fe8a55047520" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>Delete</strong> ‚Üí Delete underlying storage automatically</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8052-ab80-fafae59b1e2b"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-806b-b16a-d0e666bf58f7" class=""><strong>Key Points</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80c0-9b04-c408f055f1ec" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">PV = <strong>storage resource</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8087-b4a5-ebf3fc64d951" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">PVC = <strong>request by Pod for storage</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80af-a754-cbaa1ac8706d" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Decouples <strong>storage provisioning from Pod lifecycle</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8022-ac47-ff32237819ff" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Supports <strong>dynamic provisioning</strong> via StorageClasses</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80d1-a6ff-fc78b2e66e43"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80a9-ba9a-ed1aec237341" class=""><strong>Analogy</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8013-8c7e-c79d9f1711ff" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">PV = <strong>warehouse üì¶</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8039-9610-ce6e31d13ff8" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">PVC = <strong>order for warehouse space üìù</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80a5-bb1a-eccd45bbc710" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Pod = <strong>worker using the storage</strong></li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8092-a21e-ead74d7073f6"/><p id="272378cb-b17f-802d-bb96-cd0d30bc4324" class="">‚úÖ <strong>One-liner interview answer:</strong></p><p id="272378cb-b17f-80ca-a583-d05ffa86825a" class=""><em>Kubernetes manages storage using PersistentVolumes as cluster-level resources and PersistentVolumeClaims as Pod-level requests, allowing dynamic, decoupled, and persistent storage for stateful applications.</em></p></details></li></ul><ul id="26b378cb-b17f-8044-ae45-e02f4cec2161" class="toggle"><li><details open=""><summary><strong>Question 86:</strong> What is the purpose of a <code>Kubernetes Horizontal Pod Autoscaler</code>?</summary><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8084-986b-f7e866bae754" class=""><strong>Kubernetes Horizontal Pod Autoscaler (HPA)</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8050-9a76-d0c5055e389c" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">HPA <strong>automatically scales the number of Pods</strong> in a Deployment, ReplicaSet, or StatefulSet based on <strong>observed metrics</strong>.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8070-91d7-f4d34d858ebb" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Helps maintain <strong>application performance</strong> during changing workloads.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80fe-8eff-dcc72233a279"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80ce-bd45-dcfc19fc2f85" class=""><strong>Key Features</strong></h3><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-80c4-8f42-ecdc94476e04" class="numbered-list" start="1"><li><strong>Metric-Based Scaling</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8081-af58-c03c087256c1" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Common metrics:<ul id="272378cb-b17f-80a4-9815-f909b33dca80" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:circle">CPU utilization</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80db-b8be-c0b41dca1c88" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:circle">Memory usage</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8047-86f6-d1043643ab0f" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:circle">Custom metrics (e.g., request count, queue length)</li></ul></li></ul></li></ol><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-8098-a03b-f37b39ab51d4" class="numbered-list" start="2"><li><strong>Automatic Pod Scaling</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80a4-b134-c1bb1d61e94b" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Increases Pods when load rises</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80ab-9cd4-f155315cc7b3" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Decreases Pods when load falls</li></ul></li></ol><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-80ba-9e6c-c4a6ca020934" class="numbered-list" start="3"><li><strong>Declarative Configuration</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-800e-8cf8-e4f2a4af9215" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">HPA is configured via YAML or <code>kubectl</code> command.</li></ul></li></ol><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80c7-8eb2-d5cfc8fb7132"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-806f-9e2e-c2c2219b5031" class=""><strong>Example HPA</strong></h3><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80d6-b683-ffbc97c5debb" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl autoscale deployment my-app \
  --cpu-percent=50 \
  --min=2 \
  --max=10

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-803c-bb04-da5efe336855" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">This scales <code>my-app</code> Deployment to maintain <strong>50% CPU usage</strong>, with a minimum of 2 Pods and a maximum of 10 Pods.</li></ul><p id="272378cb-b17f-8095-a552-fe3d17ef6133" class=""><strong>YAML Example:</strong></p><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80fc-b3d9-e852eaffabc7" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: my-app-hpa
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: my-app
  minReplicas: 2
  maxReplicas: 10
  metrics:
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: cpu
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 50

</code></pre><hr id="272378cb-b17f-804b-8f76-de7fb2cd8ffd"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8074-8079-c3a0a75992ef" class=""><strong>Key Points</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8073-94d6-cdef93e08ac9" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">HPA <strong>scales Pods horizontally</strong>, not nodes.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80f8-a37d-d0e214c4a6d5" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Works with <strong>metrics-server</strong> or Prometheus Adapter for custom metrics.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-808c-96ba-e233b6926935" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Ensures <strong>high availability and efficient resource use</strong>.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8034-9aea-cbe32eee36f2"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8054-886a-fb1bf7c2f768" class=""><strong>Analogy</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80b9-813b-cc7f09846e2a" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">HPA = <strong>automatic crowd control üö¶</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80bd-89db-d6771396d5c2" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:circle">Adds more service counters (Pods) when many customers arrive and removes them when traffic decreases.</li></ul></li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80a9-8468-d6f949304394"/><p id="272378cb-b17f-8054-811e-ec67fd14bcc8" class="">‚úÖ <strong>One-liner interview answer:</strong></p><p id="272378cb-b17f-8051-bdd7-d500c2350772" class=""><em>A Kubernetes Horizontal Pod Autoscaler automatically scales the number of Pods in a Deployment, ReplicaSet, or StatefulSet based on observed metrics like CPU or memory, ensuring optimal performance under varying loads.</em></p></details></li></ul><ul id="26b378cb-b17f-8054-bcc4-c45db28a32ab" class="toggle"><li><details open=""><summary><strong>Question 87:</strong> Explain the concept of <code>Kubernetes pod affinity</code> and <code>anti-affinity</code>.</summary><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-801d-9887-f3e425cff333" class=""><strong>Kubernetes Pod Affinity &amp; Anti-Affinity</strong></h3><p id="272378cb-b17f-80f9-b480-ec6320f6e362" class=""><strong>Pod Affinity</strong> and <strong>Anti-Affinity</strong> allow you to <strong>influence where Pods are scheduled</strong> based on the labels of other Pods.</p><hr id="272378cb-b17f-805b-952a-d531608426fb"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80a7-9f24-ecb33dd1fb54" class=""><strong>1. Pod Affinity</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8022-b385-dfc293f1b8b2" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Ensures a Pod is <strong>scheduled on the same node or zone as other Pods</strong> with specific labels.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8064-8f4e-f6a846ae4155" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Useful for <strong>co-locating related Pods</strong> for low-latency communication.</li></ul><p id="272378cb-b17f-8042-b0fe-c037649c2d40" class=""><strong>Example:</strong></p><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80dd-8808-e8c33f1b255e" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">affinity:
  podAffinity:
    requiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
      - labelSelector:
          matchLabels:
            app: frontend
        topologyKey: &quot;kubernetes.io/hostname&quot;

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8017-b4ef-f712342aaa4c" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">This schedules the Pod <strong>on a node that already has Pods with label </strong><code><strong>app=frontend</strong></code>.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80f9-883f-fc4eb3f28adc"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80a9-bd44-d5b8af922d55" class=""><strong>2. Pod Anti-Affinity</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80e5-8183-ce9a32df20c1" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Ensures a Pod is <strong>not scheduled on the same node or zone as other Pods</strong> with specific labels.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8090-9998-f86b27949ee2" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Useful for <strong>spreading Pods</strong> for high availability or fault tolerance.</li></ul><p id="272378cb-b17f-80af-9667-f06d157cd110" class=""><strong>Example:</strong></p><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80c2-8e99-e858f1d24e67" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">affinity:
  podAntiAffinity:
    requiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
      - labelSelector:
          matchLabels:
            app: frontend
        topologyKey: &quot;kubernetes.io/hostname&quot;

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80c8-a56f-f813fb1523e5" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">This schedules the Pod <strong>away from nodes that already have Pods with label </strong><code><strong>app=frontend</strong></code>.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8063-84ef-de19b194619a"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-805d-a7ca-caa1c5fbc8c5" class=""><strong>Key Points</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80fc-8438-c4c146a67008" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><code><strong>topologyKey</strong></code> defines the scope (node, zone, region).</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-809e-a894-ec0922094cc6" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>Required vs Preferred</strong>:<ul id="272378cb-b17f-8041-b282-ddb7963274c3" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:circle"><code>requiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution</code> ‚Üí must satisfy the rule.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-801c-9249-ca700545b5de" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:circle"><code>preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution</code> ‚Üí best effort, but not mandatory.</li></ul></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80e8-b9ff-f7575c12b4f1" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Helps with <strong>latency optimization, fault tolerance, and workload distribution</strong>.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80ea-b473-ead2884124d7"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8072-8968-c8e482cf8900" class=""><strong>Analogy</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-801c-8b87-c9a7abbe92e4" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Pod Affinity = <strong>sit together with friends ü™ë</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8076-97ab-e957807f9540" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Pod Anti-Affinity = <strong>avoid sitting next to certain people ‚ùå</strong></li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-807f-951a-ca7ee7135d43"/><p id="272378cb-b17f-805c-8ca3-d8b75ee72fc8" class="">‚úÖ <strong>One-liner interview answer:</strong></p><p id="272378cb-b17f-8016-a74e-dfdf16ffeb8b" class=""><em>Kubernetes pod affinity schedules Pods close to other Pods with specific labels for performance or locality, while anti-affinity ensures Pods are placed apart for high availability and fault tolerance.</em></p></details></li></ul><ul id="26b378cb-b17f-8069-a168-f4a6d71bde16" class="toggle"><li><details open=""><summary><strong>Question 88:</strong> What is the difference between <code>Kubernetes job</code> and <code>Kubernetes cronjob</code>?</summary><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-801f-86bd-d80ea389591b" class=""><strong>Kubernetes Job vs CronJob</strong></h3><table id="272378cb-b17f-8082-afba-e48564b71e29" class="simple-table"><thead class="simple-table-header"><tr id="272378cb-b17f-80b8-9e57-e3b79325889c"><th id="S}tY" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header"><strong>Aspect</strong></th><th id="&lt;:XG" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header"><strong>Job</strong></th><th id=":lpa" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header"><strong>CronJob</strong></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8082-bb42-d02d4ff85a4e"><td id="S}tY" class=""><strong>Purpose</strong></td><td id="&lt;:XG" class="">Runs a <strong>one-time batch task</strong></td><td id=":lpa" class="">Runs <strong>scheduled tasks</strong> at specified times</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-80cd-ab4a-d20405e6679d"><td id="S}tY" class=""><strong>Execution</strong></td><td id="&lt;:XG" class="">Executes immediately when created</td><td id=":lpa" class="">Executes <strong>repeatedly based on a cron schedule</strong></td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-80d9-85b7-dc1328833b07"><td id="S}tY" class=""><strong>Spec</strong></td><td id="&lt;:XG" class=""><code>spec.completions</code> defines how many Pods run</td><td id=":lpa" class=""><code>spec.schedule</code> defines the cron expression</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-80cb-81b0-c095599bc63f"><td id="S}tY" class=""><strong>Lifecycle</strong></td><td id="&lt;:XG" class="">Ends when all Pods complete successfully</td><td id=":lpa" class="">Creates Jobs automatically according to schedule</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8045-bad7-e167ecc1525e"><td id="S}tY" class=""><strong>Use Case</strong></td><td id="&lt;:XG" class="">Database migration, one-time script</td><td id=":lpa" class="">Backups, periodic reports, cleanup tasks</td></tr></tbody></table><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80aa-952e-ee275d54f54c"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8028-b612-f7823f02934e" class=""><strong>Example Job</strong></h3><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8055-9b70-edffa6284653" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">apiVersion: batch/v1
kind: Job
metadata:
  name: example-job
spec:
  template:
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: job
        image: busybox
        command: [&quot;echo&quot;, &quot;Hello World&quot;]
      restartPolicy: Never
  backoffLimit: 4

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8016-8e3e-cf859d03db86" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Runs <strong>once</strong>, Pod exits after completion.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-807d-b06a-e0f5f9bf8462"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8064-9577-da4510afdbd9" class=""><strong>Example CronJob</strong></h3><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8040-9686-e77acbea123c" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">apiVersion: batch/v1
kind: CronJob
metadata:
  name: example-cronjob
spec:
  schedule: &quot;0 2 * * *&quot; # Runs daily at 2 AM
  jobTemplate:
    spec:
      template:
        spec:
          containers:
          - name: cron
            image: busybox
            command: [&quot;echo&quot;, &quot;Hello Cron&quot;]
          restartPolicy: OnFailure

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80f1-8634-da478adbd5fb" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Runs <strong>repeatedly</strong> based on the cron schedule.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80ef-8e1a-d410fa4415e9"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80f7-80d4-c15ee9749a5d" class=""><strong>Key Points</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8019-9d7b-e5ddb85f6abd" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Job = <strong>one-time execution</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80a2-a33b-e5a0ffc0845d" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">CronJob = <strong>scheduled/repeating execution</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80db-949a-f7cee9c88069" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Both are <strong>Pods that run to completion</strong>, not long-running services.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80fe-ae06-cff0cd01fb45"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80df-94cc-cf2fe143022b" class=""><strong>Analogy</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-801f-8380-c730e11f762e" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Job = <strong>send a single email ‚úâÔ∏è</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-809a-b15e-e9be179ed628" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">CronJob = <strong>send daily newsletter üì∞</strong></li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80cb-b276-d9cf6ddf8839"/><p id="272378cb-b17f-80a6-9fc2-facde945277c" class="">‚úÖ <strong>One-liner interview answer:</strong></p><p id="272378cb-b17f-8017-b53c-f7d5f0db91bf" class=""><em>A Kubernetes Job runs a one-time task to completion, while a CronJob runs Jobs on a scheduled, recurring basis according to a cron expression.</em></p></details></li></ul><ul id="26b378cb-b17f-80b5-9dce-d955dad42ad1" class="toggle"><li><details open=""><summary><strong>Question 89:</strong> How do you perform a rolling update in Kubernetes?</summary><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-809b-9c06-f3fbc3bcd846" class=""><strong>Rolling Update in Kubernetes</strong></h3><p id="272378cb-b17f-800f-bc9c-d9461a1ca3a6" class="">A <strong>rolling update</strong> gradually replaces Pods in a Deployment with new ones, ensuring <strong>continuous availability</strong>.</p><hr id="272378cb-b17f-800f-8b44-ccafb7186527"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80c2-9a7e-c29b86090849" class=""><strong>Steps to Perform a Rolling Update</strong></h3><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80cb-bb3d-ef1373487284" class=""><strong>1. Update Deployment Image</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80a3-b103-d3cf06b57be7" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Edit the Deployment YAML with the new container image:</li></ul><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8006-a3b2-c33af71e04c4" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">spec:
  containers:
  - name: my-app
    image: my-app:v2

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8056-a446-e66d644f347b" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Apply the changes:</li></ul><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-800d-b4fa-fc93467ce399" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl apply -f deployment.yaml

</code></pre><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80bb-af21-ef27a14befbb" class=""><strong>2. Check Rollout Status</strong></h3><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80b8-a7b3-ef13ca048e74" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl rollout status deployment/my-app

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8068-932b-fdc2e432eb61" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Ensures <strong>new Pods are running and ready</strong>.</li></ul><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-801e-8f62-f1e7257348e3" class=""><strong>3. Pause and Resume Rollout</strong> (Optional)</h3><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8031-bed1-c818f8c0838a" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl rollout pause deployment/my-app
kubectl rollout resume deployment/my-app

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80fc-b980-c01baedfd9af" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Useful for <strong>manual verification or stepwise updates</strong>.</li></ul><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80ee-9df0-cfd269632b7a" class=""><strong>4. Rollback if Needed</strong></h3><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8062-b0a8-e135f0c35c8f" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl rollout undo deployment/my-app

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8093-b75e-f44c26c00dca" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Reverts to the <strong>previous stable version</strong>.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8020-864a-dddf43efd9b2"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8093-b2a7-f53d820674b1" class=""><strong>Rolling Update Parameters</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80e8-a434-e4a0cb6320d3" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>maxUnavailable</strong> ‚Üí Number of Pods that can be unavailable during update.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-807f-83e0-ec661291afd4" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>maxSurge</strong> ‚Üí Number of extra Pods created above desired replicas during update.</li></ul><p id="272378cb-b17f-8085-bbf7-ee6219affe25" class=""><strong>Example in YAML:</strong></p><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8092-a5ea-e9aa4f55abe5" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">strategy:
  type: RollingUpdate
  rollingUpdate:
    maxSurge: 1
    maxUnavailable: 0

</code></pre><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8056-a9b9-e8601e42fe24"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8049-9be6-d8a1d2cf0b99" class=""><strong>Key Points</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8086-954f-c474f834b9c3" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Ensures <strong>zero-downtime deployment</strong>.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80a2-a869-f2087e840939" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Kubernetes <strong>gradually terminates old Pods and brings up new Pods</strong>.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80e5-b92e-d4a60ca79728" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Works <strong>automatically for Deployments</strong>; StatefulSets have their own update strategy.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80d7-8a41-c5d2ab5286f8"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-801c-b7e3-d9afc6eb9f8a" class=""><strong>Analogy</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8070-a896-d61b21b11a4c" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Rolling update = <strong>replacing old light bulbs one at a time üí°</strong><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8071-b993-d27e643c8f2b" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:circle">Ensures the room remains lit throughout the process.</li></ul></li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-803f-8161-ea03127e92a4"/><p id="272378cb-b17f-8078-93cd-d7feb3ec9f59" class="">‚úÖ <strong>One-liner interview answer:</strong></p><p id="272378cb-b17f-80d3-ad3d-fc0ad2d6e194" class=""><em>A Kubernetes rolling update gradually replaces old Pods with new ones in a Deployment, ensuring zero downtime, with parameters for max surge and max unavailable Pods.</em></p></details></li></ul><ul id="26b378cb-b17f-80c5-8027-f2342ef7075a" class="toggle"><li><details open=""><summary><strong>Question 90:</strong> What are the different types of Kubernetes services and their use cases?</summary><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8008-bb41-d059cb6eb509" class=""><strong>Kubernetes Services</strong></h3><p id="272378cb-b17f-801c-a23d-d9d1a08bd935" class="">A <strong>Service</strong> is an abstraction that defines a <strong>logical set of Pods</strong> and a <strong>policy to access them</strong>. Services provide <strong>stable IPs and DNS names</strong>, even if Pod IPs change.</p><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8049-ab82-d0cbcbf264b6"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-805b-bb99-f6d3ad228012" class=""><strong>Types of Services and Use Cases</strong></h3><table id="272378cb-b17f-808e-8388-e5dbd8d8d2eb" class="simple-table"><thead class="simple-table-header"><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8071-9399-e5df274e1f00"><th id="{hRH" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header"><strong>Service Type</strong></th><th id="&lt;CI`" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header" style="width:275px"><strong>Description</strong></th><th id="vjLY" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header" style="width:271px"><strong>Use Case</strong></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr id="272378cb-b17f-801b-a4db-eb112b10d850"><td id="{hRH" class=""><strong>ClusterIP</strong> (default)</td><td id="&lt;CI`" class="" style="width:275px">Exposes Service <strong>internally</strong> within the cluster only.</td><td id="vjLY" class="" style="width:271px">Internal communication between Pods; e.g., backend APIs.</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-80ec-80e1-ea8b6bb78d1c"><td id="{hRH" class=""><strong>NodePort</strong></td><td id="&lt;CI`" class="" style="width:275px">Exposes Service on <strong>each Node‚Äôs IP at a static port</strong>.</td><td id="vjLY" class="" style="width:271px">Quick external access for testing or development.</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8017-8cea-cfcceeb9028b"><td id="{hRH" class=""><strong>LoadBalancer</strong></td><td id="&lt;CI`" class="" style="width:275px">Creates a <strong>cloud provider load balancer</strong> that routes external traffic.</td><td id="vjLY" class="" style="width:271px">Production workloads needing external access; e.g., web apps.</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-80fa-b4e1-f29f074755a7"><td id="{hRH" class=""><strong>ExternalName</strong></td><td id="&lt;CI`" class="" style="width:275px">Maps Service to an <strong>external DNS name</strong>.</td><td id="vjLY" class="" style="width:271px">Access external services via a Kubernetes Service.</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8096-8f26-dfdb2f419357"><td id="{hRH" class=""><strong>Headless Service</strong></td><td id="&lt;CI`" class="" style="width:275px"><strong>No ClusterIP</strong>; used for direct Pod-to-Pod communication.</td><td id="vjLY" class="" style="width:271px">Stateful applications, like databases, with DNS-based service discovery.</td></tr></tbody></table><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8078-a54a-cc86a8d6ef7c"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8085-aebf-f63adc016467" class=""><strong>Example: ClusterIP Service</strong></h3><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8053-85b4-f7bcb9ddfadc" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: my-service
spec:
  selector:
    app: my-app
  ports:
    - protocol: TCP
      port: 80
      targetPort: 8080
  type: ClusterIP

</code></pre><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80d2-bb3e-d858a23fb508"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8091-ab63-d5f27e470d3b" class=""><strong>Key Points</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8007-8182-d28a432b5a9c" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>ClusterIP</strong> ‚Üí Internal-only, default.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80cb-8113-d95479f00c34" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>NodePort</strong> ‚Üí Simple external access, exposes on <code>&lt;NodeIP&gt;:&lt;NodePort&gt;</code>.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8063-8e21-f4fcdb28a4b1" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>LoadBalancer</strong> ‚Üí Production-ready external access via cloud LB.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80a2-9312-c70cc42c0c31" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>ExternalName</strong> ‚Üí Alias to external DNS service.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80be-b0d9-cfe8c8f0abe6" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>Headless</strong> ‚Üí No ClusterIP, used for StatefulSets and direct Pod discovery.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8077-95b7-f6bd5000363b"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8044-b684-c17e04451982" class=""><strong>Analogy</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80b1-aa28-f8a126244563" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">ClusterIP = <strong>internal office phone üìû</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80df-b725-d1354013e20f" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">NodePort = <strong>doorbell at each building entrance üö™</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-803c-b61a-fd35f3e2f09c" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">LoadBalancer = <strong>reception desk directing visitors üè¢</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-803d-9c8c-f6c706b3630f" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">ExternalName = <strong>forwarding to external office üåê</strong></li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-803e-a887-f99dcaa00185" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Headless = <strong>direct phone lines to each employee ‚òéÔ∏è</strong></li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80fd-9986-f76d48bedd27"/><p id="272378cb-b17f-805f-ab87-fd273339fde1" class="">‚úÖ <strong>One-liner interview answer:</strong></p><p id="272378cb-b17f-80a9-8e6c-d5c91f904c75" class=""><em>Kubernetes Services types include ClusterIP (internal), NodePort (external via node port), LoadBalancer (cloud LB), ExternalName (DNS alias), and Headless (direct Pod discovery), each serving different communication and exposure needs.</em></p></details></li></ul><ul id="26b378cb-b17f-808d-bdaf-dbee46a8ebc1" class="toggle"><li><details open=""><summary><strong>Question 91:</strong> What is the purpose of Kubernetes <code>liveness probes</code> and <code>readiness probes</code>?</summary><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80af-a9ac-f332dac8d825" class=""><strong>1. Liveness Probe</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8040-8562-e5b10f66be3f" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>Checks if a container is alive</strong>.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-802f-98d8-ee7c2e7862c0" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">If the container is <strong>unhealthy</strong>, Kubernetes <strong>restarts it</strong> automatically.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80f1-b06a-e87e1f8cdbdd" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Helps <strong>recover from deadlocks or crashes</strong>.</li></ul><p id="272378cb-b17f-80f1-8509-c6d88865ae0a" class=""><strong>Example:</strong></p><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80ec-a1b3-c81986874419" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">livenessProbe:
  httpGet:
    path: /healthz
    port: 8080
  initialDelaySeconds: 5
  periodSeconds: 10

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8087-a2ee-f6c32067013b" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Kubernetes makes an HTTP request to <code>/healthz</code> every 10 seconds.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80ca-a32e-c90503bdac3d" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">If it fails, the Pod is <strong>restarted</strong>.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80cf-9f27-dfd80ed76c11"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80c2-9d12-cdb1de40db2b" class=""><strong>2. Readiness Probe</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-808f-8d3a-ff6227872666" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>Checks if a container is ready to serve traffic</strong>.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-800b-99f6-e9ebf936293a" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">If it fails, Kubernetes <strong>removes the Pod from the Service endpoints</strong> temporarily.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8070-a3be-f75acffa8b20" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Ensures <strong>traffic is only sent to ready Pods</strong>.</li></ul><p id="272378cb-b17f-802b-bef6-e321e04f6008" class=""><strong>Example:</strong></p><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-808c-8630-efa2b07e4239" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">readinessProbe:
  httpGet:
    path: /ready
    port: 8080
  initialDelaySeconds: 5
  periodSeconds: 10

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-801c-909c-c1668f56308e" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">If <code>/ready</code> fails, the Pod <strong>stays alive but won‚Äôt receive traffic</strong>.</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-803e-97f7-d1db9a03f59b"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8081-9dc9-f1a5d1140968" class=""><strong>Key Differences</strong></h3><table id="272378cb-b17f-8074-b84d-ea72cfc1b280" class="simple-table"><thead class="simple-table-header"><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8091-8c9b-ecaa84c131f5"><th id="q`hX" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header"><strong>Aspect</strong></th><th id="GPmD" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header"><strong>Liveness Probe</strong></th><th id="`}g:" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header"><strong>Readiness Probe</strong></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr id="272378cb-b17f-80ab-83b7-f99247487dd8"><td id="q`hX" class=""><strong>Purpose</strong></td><td id="GPmD" class="">Check if container is alive</td><td id="`}g:" class="">Check if container is ready to serve traffic</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-80c0-8b1c-ef4f2d5f4bf0"><td id="q`hX" class=""><strong>Action on Failure</strong></td><td id="GPmD" class="">Restart the container</td><td id="`}g:" class="">Remove from Service endpoints temporarily</td></tr><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8006-959a-d19c9a9261b5"><td id="q`hX" class=""><strong>Use Case</strong></td><td id="GPmD" class="">Detect deadlocks or crashes</td><td id="`}g:" class="">Prevent sending traffic to uninitialized containers</td></tr></tbody></table><hr id="272378cb-b17f-8088-b59b-ed3aec59abdd"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-80fe-a42c-cca43dd2cc25" class=""><strong>Analogy</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80fd-9fee-d47b512bdddf" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Liveness = <strong>checking if a worker is awake üò¥</strong> (restart if asleep)</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-801f-a920-d18d890730ef" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Readiness = <strong>checking if a worker is ready to handle tasks ‚úÖ</strong> (don‚Äôt assign work until ready)</li></ul><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80a6-995f-f5a7b8b4a6be"/><p id="272378cb-b17f-8024-8e49-d7cd54f64168" class="">‚úÖ <strong>One-liner interview answer:</strong></p><p id="272378cb-b17f-8051-85cb-c8fed221b3f6" class=""><em>Kubernetes liveness probes detect if a container is alive and restart it if needed, while readiness probes check if a container is ready to serve traffic and remove it from Service endpoints if not.</em></p></details></li></ul><ul id="26b378cb-b17f-80f9-8b20-c1bea2097350" class="toggle"><li><details open=""><summary><strong>Question 92:</strong> Explain how Kubernetes handles rolling updates and rollbacks.</summary><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8009-8992-f9c010706cfb" class=""><strong>Kubernetes Rolling Updates</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80af-acb9-e87808599932" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc"><strong>Rolling Update</strong> gradually replaces old Pods with new ones in a Deployment or StatefulSet, ensuring <strong>zero downtime</strong>.</li></ul><ul id="272378cb-b17f-8073-9a42-fab44aac13ad" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Kubernetes maintains the <strong>desired number of replicas</strong> during the update.</li></ul><p id="272378cb-b17f-8095-8b19-f05db80e5be8" class=""><strong>Steps for Rolling Update:</strong></p><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-8071-b07f-e912e74f7663" class="numbered-list" start="1"><li><strong>Update Deployment Manifest</strong></li></ol><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80e4-b7de-fe3fdb16cd32" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-YAML" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">spec:
  containers:
  - name: my-app
    image: my-app:v2

</code></pre><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-80fc-bd76-e2048ef26a7f" class="numbered-list" start="1"><li><strong>Apply the Update</strong></li></ol><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80e8-b0f5-c2ae38c5e4a9" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl apply -f deployment.yaml

</code></pre><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-808e-abc3-dae47fd5bcd2" class="numbered-list" start="1"><li><strong>Monitor Rollout</strong></li></ol><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80a1-bcbb-d4f74ba60dbb" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl rollout status deployment/my-app

</code></pre><ol type="1" id="272378cb-b17f-802e-a33b-cb90baf1983b" class="numbered-list" start="1"><li><strong>Control Rollout</strong></li></ol><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80be-bfbd-c16e35609ecb" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Pause rollout:</li></ul><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-809a-bad5-f8a92e5eedbe" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl rollout pause deployment/my-app

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80c3-99d1-c837fb7fbd72" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">Resume rollout:</li></ul><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80bf-a599-c32949fcebf3" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl rollout resume deployment/my-app

</code></pre><hr id="272378cb-b17f-80c8-92c6-cacb75961816"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-800b-8cea-edba01384cd7" class=""><strong>Kubernetes Rollback</strong></h3><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80c6-a37c-f157c04e3a15" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">If a rollout fails, Kubernetes allows <strong>rollback to the previous stable version</strong>.</li></ul><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-80f6-b496-d23ca4115133" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl rollout undo deployment/my-app

</code></pre><ul id="272378cb-b17f-80ae-acc7-f2a5446b4cad" class="bulleted-list"><li style="list-style-type:disc">You can also <strong>rollback to a specific revision</strong>:</li></ul><script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/prism.min.js" integrity="sha512-7Z9J3l1+EYfeaPKcGXu3MS/7T+w19WtKQY/n+xzmw4hZhJ9tyYmcUS+4QqAlzhicE5LAfMQSF3iFTK9bQdTxXg==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"></script><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/prism/1.29.0/themes/prism.min.css" integrity="sha512-tN7Ec6zAFaVSG3TpNAKtk4DOHNpSwKHxxrsiw4GHKESGPs5njn/0sMCUMl2svV4wo4BK/rCP7juYz+zx+l6oeQ==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/><pre id="272378cb-b17f-8012-bfd4-e7e8ec92ff57" class="code code-wrap"><code class="language-Bash" style="white-space:pre-wrap;word-break:break-all">kubectl rollout undo deployment/my-app --to-revision=2

</code></pre><hr id="272378cb-b17f-807e-bb24-f11167222222"/><h3 id="272378cb-b17f-8026-bfc9-e948cb069eba" class=""><strong>Update Strategies</strong></h3><table id="272378cb-b17f-8083-8351-d684136af43f" class="simple-table"><thead class="simple-table-header"><tr id="272378cb-b17f-8040-a77e-c14b714ddfee"><th id="_;Cr" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header"><strong>Strategy</strong></th><th id="]h|q" class="simple-table-header-color simple-table-header"><strong>Description</strong></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr id="272378cb-b17f-802a-9d4e-c9e65ecdde33"><td id="_;Cr" class=""><strong>RollingUpdate</strong></td><td id="]h|q" class="">Gradually replaces Pods while maintaining availability</td></tr><tr
